		Initial						Size = XYZ(random(0.300, 0.500), random(0.300, 0.500), random(0.300, 0.500))
		Initial						Rotate = XYZ(random(0, 360), random(0, 360), random(0, 360))
	}
	eventsequence "A_RRF_LIMIT_CRUSHER_P05"
	{
		particleType		= PT_3D_PLANE
		Emitrate			= 10
		Lifetime			= 0.300
		NumParticles		= 10
		TriggerTime			= 1.260
		DrawCount			= 2
		Layer				= 14
		Gravity				= XYZ(random(-30, 30), random(0, 20), random(-30, 30))
		BillBoardType		= BT_ALL
		SourceBlendMode	= D3DBLEND_SRCALPHA
		DestBlendMode	= D3DBLEND_DESTALPHA
		Trace				= TRUE
		ZEnable				= FALSE

		Initial						Texture = "Particle_Blur.dds"
		Initial						Color = RGBA(1, 1, 1, 0)
		Fade so From 0.001 to 0.033	Color = RGBA(1, 0.500, 0.200, random(0.600, 1))
		Fade so From 0.100 to 0.300	Color = RGBA(random(0.500, 1), 0, random(0.500, 1), 0)
		Initial						Size = XYZ(random(40, 50), random(40, 50), 1)
		Fade so From 0.010 to 0.300	Size = XYZ(random(130, 150), random(130, 150), 1)
		Initial						Scale = random(0.800, 1.200)
	}
